    <article class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article">
     <div class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_label">
      <span class="trb_outfit_categorySectionHeading">

     <h2 class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_title trb_outfit_featuredArticleTitle">
      <a href="/news/local/allentown/mc-creative-minds-daycare-certificate-revoked-20161130-story.html#nt=oft12aH-2la1" class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_title_a">
       State revokes certificate for Allentown day care where profane video was created
      </a>
      <span class="trb_outfits_metabuckets">
       <span class="trb_outfits_metabuckets_1">
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
    </article>
   </section>
   <p class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_content">
    <span class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_content_text">
     ALLENTOWN â€” Pennsylvania&apos;s Department of Human Services has decided to revoke the license of the Allentown day care center where a video was created of a staff member encouraging children to curse.   The day care demonstrated &quot;gross incompetence and negligence in the operation of a child care program,&quot;...
    </span>
   </p>
